                                            <div class="intro-text intro">

            <h1 class="_title post-title intro__title">PhD in Disability Studies</h1>
    
            <p class="_subtitle intro__subtitle">Promoting the full participation, self-determination and equal citizenship of people with disabilities</p>
    
        <div class="intro__text"><p>Disability studies scholars view disability not simply as a defect inside a person, but as a complex relationship between society and people who function differently from the norm.</p>
<p>UIC&#8217;s PhD in disability studies program addresses disability in its full complexity, promoting an awareness of disability that supports individuals in shaping their identities and lives<span class="redactor-invisible-space">. We examine how support services and social and political change can reduce sources of disempowerment.</span></p>
<p>Disability studies at UIC offers a unique opportunity to study the multilayered, interactional dynamics<span class="redactor-invisible-space"> </span>of disability.</p>
</div>
    
</div>
                    
                                            <div class="content-sections">

</div>
    
    
    

    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
            <h3 class="subsection-header">Interdisciplinary Experience</h3>
    
    

    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
            <div class="richtext-component text component component-text-block"><p><span class="redactor-invisible-space">Our program is truly an interdisciplinary experience, with faculty, researchers, and students coming from backgrounds in health, education, assistive technology, social sciences and humanities. </span>We recognize the inherent tensions that exist between therapeutic, medical and social models of disability, but acknowledge these differences as fertile ground for the development of disability studies as an integrative knowledge base.</p>
</div>
    
    
    
    
    

    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
            <div class="quote-component component">
    <blockquote class="blockquote-component">
        <div class="_quote">I really benefitted from the interdisciplinary nature of the program, which gave me new ways of understanding and experiencing disability.</div>

                

    <div class="_citation">
                    <span class="_author">
  Jenna Heffron 
  </span>
                            &nbsp;|&nbsp;
                            <span class="_description">
  PhD ‘16 
  </span>
            </div>

    </blockquote>
</div>
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    </div>

</div>
                                                            <div class="section">

    <h2 class="section__title">Your career</h2>

    <div class="section__components">
        
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
            <div class="richtext-component text component component-text-block"><p>Students enroll in our program for a variety of reasons and with a variety of goals for when they graduate, including academic positions, disability policy and advocacy, and visual or performing arts.</p>
<p>A PhD in disability studies gives you advanced knowledge about complex social implications of disability. You&#8217;ll develop the skills to lead research, policy analysis, and program evaluation and development in ways that best address the perspectives of people with disabilities.</p>
</div>

                                                            <div class="section">

    <h2 class="section__title">DHD Connections</h2>

    <div class="section__components">
        
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
            <div class="richtext-component text component component-text-block"><p>Our program provides you with the opportunity to embrace interdisciplinary education beyond the classroom and link to the disability community.  By joining DHD you will become a part of our collaborative network of diverse faculty, staff, students, and partners including people with disabilities, family members, organizations, academic departments and universities in Illinois, nationally and internationally.  Build your experience through DHD connections:</p>
<ul>
<li>Engage with the community through collaboration and field experiences in the disability sector</li>
<li>Participate in research or teaching through an assistantship</li>
<li>Share your knowledge by training others and presenting at conferences</li>
<li>Produce scholarly publications that contribute to the scientific knowledge base on disability</li>
</ul>
<p>Some of our past students have worked in policy positions at legal and government centers in Washington, D.C., learning about policy-making processes that affect the lives of disabled citizens and their families. Others have traveled internationally to conduct research, present papers, and participate in service initiatives as they learn how the disability studies knowledge base can expand to incorporate experiences of disability in many cultures.</p>
</div>
    
    
    
    
    

    
    
    
    
    
            <div class="component highlight component-highlight-image">

    <div class="_image">
        <div class="highlight__image">
